Angle;cut;>;space;;space;**Step 1: Identify the lines in the image.**;space;;space;The two lines in the image are given as $\overline{AB}$ and $\overline{CD}.$;space;;space;**Step 2: Calculate the angle between the lines.**;space;;space;To find the angle between the lines, we can use the dot product formula for two vectors $\vec{a}$ and $\vec{b}$:;space;;space;$$\vec{a} \cdot \vec{b} = |\vec{a}| |\vec{b}| \cos \theta$$;space;;space;where $\theta$ is the angle between the two vectors.;space;;space;**Step 3: Apply the dot product formula.**;space;;space;Let $\vec{a} = \overrightarrow{AB}$ and $\vec{b} = \overrightarrow{CD}.$ Then, we have:;space;;space;$$\overrightarrow{AB} \cdot \overrightarrow{CD} = |\overrightarrow{AB}| |\overrightarrow{CD}| \cos \theta$$;space;;space;We can calculate the magnitudes of the vectors:;space;;space;$$|\overrightarrow{AB}| = \sqrt{(-3)^2 + 4^2} = 5$$;space;;space;$$|\overrightarrow{CD}| = \sqrt{4^2 + 3^2} = 5$$;space;;space;Substituting these values into the equation, we get:;space;;space;$$\overrightarrow{AB} \cdot \overrightarrow{CD} = 5 \cdot 5 \cos \theta$$;space;;space;**Step 4: Solve for $\theta$.**;space;;space;We know that $\overrightarrow{AB} \cdot \overrightarrow{CD} = -1$, so we can solve for $\theta$:;space;;space;$$-1 = 25 \cos \theta$$;space;;space;$$\cos \theta = -\frac{1}{25}$$;space;;space;$$\theta = \cos^{-1} \left(-\frac{1}{25}\right)$$;space;;space;Using a calculator, we find that $\theta \approx 78.46^\circ$.;space;;space;**Final answer:**;space;;space;Therefore, the angle between the two lines is approximately $\boxed{78}$ degrees.<|eot_id|>;cut;(a) 39 degrees
